  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{

  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

ghost function Sum(s: seq<int>): int

}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}
```

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    // Ensure that the sum of the first i elements of a and b is known
    assert Sum(a[..i]) == Sum(a[..i]);
    assert Sum(b[..i]) == Sum(b[..i]);

    // Update current occupancy using the known sums
    current := Sum(b[..i]) - Sum(a[..i]);

    // After updating current, ensure it matches the loop invariant
    assert current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i]);

    // Now incorporate the next stop
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);

    // Update current to include the new stop
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum([x]) == x; // by definition
    assert Sum(s) + x == 0 + x;
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum((s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1]) + (s + [x])[|s + [x]| - 1];
    assert Sum((s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1]) == Sum(s);
    assert (s + [x])[|s + [x]| - 1] == x;
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {

    // The following calls are necessary so that Dafny knows
    // that the sums of the prefixes are updated correctly.
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);

    // Update the current occupancy
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];

    // If the new occupancy exceeds the current capacity,
    // update the capacity.
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n

    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:

ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|

  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded

  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|

  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|

  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:

  requires |a| == |b|

{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c

  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

{

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(s: seq<int>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0 else Sum(s[..|s|-1]) + s[|s|-1]
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

  }

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    // After adding the next stop, the occupancy updates correctly
    // We assert that the current occupancy after the update equals
    // the occupancy computed from the sequences up to i+1
    var nextCurrent := current - a[i] + b[i];
    current := nextCurrent;
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    // Deriving the effect of appending a[i] and b[i] to the sequences
    // to maintain the invariants about current
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);

    // Update the current occupancy
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];

    // Update the capacity if the new occupancy exceeds the current capacity
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }

    // Advance to the next stop
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{

  capacity := 0;

    invariant capacity >= 0

  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

```dafny
ghost function Sum(s: seq<int>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0 else Sum(s[..|s|-1]) + s[|s|-1]
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;

  }

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(s: seq<int>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0 else Sum(s[..|s|-1]) + s[|s|-1]
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    assert |a| == |b|;
    assert |a[..i]| == i && |b[..i]| == i;
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}
